# PROGRESS-HISTORY.md ‚Äî KhundiConnect full build history (archive)

> This is the append-only long-form record split out of PROGRESS.md. Newest archived entries first. The live SHORT tracker is PROGRESS.md. Do not delete entries here ‚Äî this is the state-recovery record.

---

- **Build-step 66 ‚Äî Taxonomy Governance (OMJ standard taxonomy ¬∑ Khundi locals ¬∑ review queue: promote/alias/remap)** üü¢ **complete ‚Äî `[CHECKPOINT]` (continuous mode).** branch `feat/66-taxonomy-governance-v31` (off the 65 head); **WORK-TYPE: FEATURE** (new OMJ-altitude governance over option taxonomies, ARCHITECTURE ¬ß32; the build-step-49 "OMJ governs / Khundi consumes" pattern). spec `specs/66-taxonomy-governance-v31.md`, CODEREF `specs/65-69-CODEREF.md`. tests **1320/1320** (163 suites; **+35** net). **Wave 3 / item 2 ‚Äî depends on 65; foundation for 67 (census governed-domain fields) + 68/69 aggregation.** **Tenant isolation ‚úÖ + OMJ-scope test ‚úÖ** ‚Äî NEW tenant table `taxonomy_local` (RLS ENABLE+FORCE, tenant FK Cascade) + NEW global reference table `taxonomy_standard` (NO tenant_id, NO RLS, like `permissions`/`module_registry`); the ONLY cross-Khundi path is the OMJ review queue on the audited platform path, permission-gated `taxonomy.govern` @ ALL_TENANTS.
  - **The problem (spec ¬ß1).** Option sets are per-Khundi, so "education"/"occupation"/"income_band"/"relationship" values diverge across Khundis ("MBBS" vs "Doctor" vs "doctor") ‚Äî OMJ-wide aggregation is noisy. The fix governs a taxonomy WITHOUT blocking a Khundi or editing any submission: OMJ owns a STANDARD list per domain; a Khundi adds a LOCAL value INSTANTLY (no approval to USE); every local surfaces to an OMJ REVIEW QUEUE where OMJ can PROMOTE (make standard), MERGE-ALIAS (point at an existing standard) or RE-MAP it ‚Äî a read-time mapping the aggregation applies, never an edit of stored answers.
  - **Data-model decision (spec ¬ß3 / CODEREF ‚Äî "fold mapping into local").** TWO tables, not three: `taxonomy_standard` (global reference: `domain, value, label, order, active`; unique `(domain,value)`) + `taxonomy_local` (tenant data: `tenant_id, domain, value, label, status('local'|'promoted'|'aliased'|'remapped'), mapped_standard_value?, mapping_kind?('alias'|'remap'), created_by, decided_by, decided_at`; unique `(tenant_id,domain,value)`). The OMJ mapping is FOLDED into `taxonomy_local` so the only RLS surface is one tenant table ‚Äî simpler + isolation-absolute. Migration `20260714000000_taxonomy_governance`.
  - **A. Shared (`packages/shared/src/index.ts`).** `TAXONOMY_DOMAINS` (education/occupation/income_band/relationship) + `isGovernedTaxonomyDomain`; `TAXONOMY_LOCAL_STATUSES` + `TAXONOMY_MAPPING_KINDS`; views `TaxonomyStandardView`/`TaxonomyLocalView`/`TaxonomyDomainView`/`TaxonomyReviewItem`; `TAXONOMY_STANDARD_SEED` (code-seeded canonical lists, 8/9/5/11 values per domain). NEW pure, tested helpers: `resolveTaxonomyValue(value, locals)` (a decided local‚Üíits standard; un-decided/standard‚Üíitself ‚Äî read-time, never edits submissions); `applyTaxonomyMapping(values, locals)` (aggregation roll-up ‚Äî aliased/remapped fold under standard); `buildTaxonomyOptions(standard, locals)` (option-editor merge: active-standard-first, non-promoted locals, de-duped so a promoted local never doubles); `validateTaxonomyMapping(local, target, standard)` (rejects self-ref/unknown/inactive before any write). NEW permissions `taxonomy.contribute` (CORE, OWN_TENANT) + `taxonomy.govern` (OVERSIGHT, ALL_TENANTS ‚Äî added to `NON_TENANT_PERMISSION_KEYS`). Label catalog += `taxonomy_domain`/`taxonomy_status`/`taxonomy_mapping_kind`/`taxonomy_option_origin` (EN/UR). `nav.taxonomy`/`nav.taxonomyGov` (EN/UR core catalog).
  - **B. Prisma + migration (`20260714000000_taxonomy_governance`).** `taxonomy_standard` CREATE ‚Äî global reference, NO tenant_id, NO RLS. `taxonomy_local` CREATE ‚Äî `tenant_id` FK `ON DELETE CASCADE`, RLS `ENABLE` + `FORCE` with the docs/MULTITENANCY.md isolation policy (`app_rls_bypass() OR tenant_id = app_current_tenant_id()`). `Tenant.taxonomyLocals` back-relation. Seed `seedTaxonomyStandard()` upserts `TAXONOMY_STANDARD_SEED` (idempotent, global).
  - **C. API (`apps/api/src/taxonomy/`).** `taxonomy.service.ts` ‚Äî KHUNDI path (`runWithTenant`, RLS): `listDomain` (standard+own locals), `addLocal` (label-only; value auto-slugged via `slugifyFieldKey`; rejects standard-collision; idempotent on re-add; usable immediately). OMJ path (`runAsPlatform`, RLS bypass, gated `taxonomy.govern`): `reviewQueue` (pending locals across Khundis + tenant labels), `listStandard` (target picker), `promote` (upserts a standard row + stamps local promoted‚Üíself), `mapLocal` (validated alias/remap; records mapping + `decided_by`/`decided_at`). All audited (`Logger('Audit')`). `taxonomy.controller.ts` ‚Äî `TaxonomyController` (`/taxonomy/*`, OWN_TENANT `taxonomy.contribute`) + `TaxonomyPlatformController` (`/platform/taxonomy/*`, ALL_TENANTS `taxonomy.govern`). `taxonomy.dto.ts` (`AddLocalDto` label-only ‚Äî client can never set value/status/tenant; `MapLocalDto`), `taxonomy.mapper.ts`, `taxonomy.module.ts` (registered in `app.module.ts`). OMJ Admin seed role += `taxonomy.govern`; President/Gen-Sec/Councilor tenant roles += `taxonomy.contribute`.
  - **D. Web.** OMJ governance screen `apps/web/app/platform/taxonomy/page.tsx` (review queue; per-item Promote + standard-value picker + Merge/Re-map; toasts; gated `taxonomy.govern`). Khundi taxonomy panel `apps/web/app/taxonomy/page.tsx` (per-domain standard+local via `buildTaxonomyOptions`; add-a-local usable immediately; status chips; gated `taxonomy.contribute`). Nav entries: `/taxonomy` (Operations, `taxonomy.contribute`) + `/platform/taxonomy` (Platform & OMJ, `taxonomy.govern`). All labels via `formatLabel`; zero physical-direction Tailwind.
  - **Acceptance (spec ¬ß6):** (1) a Khundi adds a local + uses it immediately, no approval gate ‚úÖ. (2) the local surfaces in OMJ's queue; OMJ promotes/aliases/remaps; decision recorded; submissions never edited ‚úÖ. (3) aggregation rolls aliased/remapped locals under their standard while the Khundi keeps its local label ‚úÖ (`applyTaxonomyMapping`/`resolveTaxonomyValue` pure+tested; census/insights/report wiring over governed domains lands with 67's governed-domain census fields). (4) standard = OMJ reference (no tenant_id); locals+mapping tenant-isolated; no Khundi reads another's locals; OMJ reads across via its altitude scope only ‚úÖ. (5) migration regression + isolation absolute; OMJ-scope is the only cross-path and is permission-gated ‚úÖ. (6) gates green incl. isolation + OMJ-scope permission test + i18n ‚úÖ.
  - **Scope note (option-editor binding).** Spec ¬ß4 / CODEREF call for the build-step-65 INLINE field option editor to read `taxonomy_standard`+`taxonomy_local` for a field bound to a governed domain. A FormField has no `taxonomyDomain` binding yet ‚Äî that binding is introduced with the **build-step-67 census redesign** (Gatta-G census fields adopt governed domains, per CODEREF 67). This step ships the full governance backbone (shared contract + API + data model + both web surfaces: a dedicated Khundi taxonomy panel satisfying "Khundi sees standard+local + adds a usable local", and the OMJ governance screen); the per-field option-editor wiring lands in 67 where the domain-bound fields exist. The aggregation helpers (`applyTaxonomyMapping`) are shipped+tested so 67/68 apply them directly.
  - **Gates:** typecheck ‚úÖ (shared/api/web), lint ‚úÖ (api no warnings, web no errors), web build ‚úÖ (both new routes `/taxonomy` + `/platform/taxonomy` static), prisma validate ‚úÖ, API tests **1320/1320** (163 suites) ‚úÖ incl. i18n en‚áîur parity + web-coverage (35 new t-keys both locales + delta `i18n-deltas/taxonomy-governance.json`). NEW specs: `taxonomy-helpers.spec.ts`, `taxonomy.migration.spec.ts` (standard NO-RLS, local RLS ENABLE+FORCE, no tenant_id on standard, unique keys, cascade ‚Äî real migration chain on PGlite), `taxonomy.isolation.spec.ts` (cross-tenant read/update/delete denied, no-context deny-by-default, platform path sees all, standard readable from any context), `taxonomy.access.spec.ts` (**OMJ-scope test** ‚Äî `taxonomy.govern` ALL_TENANTS-only + in NON_TENANT_PERMISSION_KEYS + on OMJ seed role), `taxonomy.service.spec.ts` (add/idempotent/collision/ungoverned-reject/queue-spans-Khundis/promote/alias-validate/NotFound). **Isolation ‚úÖ + OMJ-scope permission test ‚úÖ.**

- **Build-step 65 ‚Äî Advanced Form Builder (inline options ¬∑ auto-slug ¬∑ new field types ¬∑ conditional logic)** üü¢ **complete ‚Äî `[CHECKPOINT]` (continuous mode).** branch `feat/65-form-builder-advanced-v31` (off the staging head after 64); **WORK-TYPE: FEATURE** (extends the build-step-20 form engine, ARCHITECTURE ¬ß32). spec `specs/65-form-builder-advanced-v31.md`, CODEREF `specs/65-69-CODEREF.md`. tests **1285/1285** (158 suites; **+23** net). **Wave 3 / item 1 ‚Äî foundation for 66 (taxonomy) + 67 (census).** **Tenant isolation ‚úÖ** ‚Äî additive enum extension + one `form_fields` ADD COLUMN; new migration regression proves enum values added (no data loss), `visibility` column nullable JSONB, form-builder RLS preserved (ENABLE+FORCE), and a visibility rule is tenant-isolated (foreign tenant cannot read/write).
  - **What shipped (the 5 gaps in spec ¬ß1):** (1) **inline options** ‚Äî an admin types choices right on a choice field; the engine creates/updates the field's `OptionSet` transparently (admin never meets "OptionSet"). (2) **auto-slug / no keys shown** ‚Äî the builder is label-first; `slugifyFieldKey(label)` derives the machine key server-side (collision-suffixed, Urdu‚Üístable hash fallback) and the key is NEVER shown. (3) **no raw enums** ‚Äî field-type + operator pickers route through `formatLabel` (new `form_field_type` rows + new `visibility_op` domain, EN/UR). (4) **new field types** ‚Äî `radio` (single-choice buttons), `checkbox` (multi-checkbox group), `member` (member picker ‚Üí stores a member id), `searchable` (typeahead single-select). (5) **conditional/cascading logic** ‚Äî a field shows only when its `visibility` rule passes; multi-level cascades resolve (a hidden parent's answer counts as unanswered).
  - **A. Shared (`packages/shared/src/index.ts`).** `FormFieldType` union + `FORM_FIELD_TYPES` += the four types; helpers `fieldTypeUsesOptions`/`fieldTypeIsMulti`. NEW pure, tested helpers: `slugifyFieldKey(label, taken)`; `FieldVisibility`/`VisibilityRule`/`VisibilityOp` + `VISIBILITY_OPS`; `evaluateFieldVisibility(field, answers)` + `visibleFields(fields, answers)` (fixpoint cascade resolution, bounded by field count); `validateVisibilityRefs(fields)` (unknown-ref / self-ref / bad-op / **cycle** via DFS colour map). `FormFieldView` += `visibility`. **`validateSubmission` now shares ONE evaluator with the web renderer** ‚Äî a field hidden by its rule is neither required nor validated; the type switch groups `select|radio|searchable` (single choice) + `multiselect|checkbox` (multi) and adds `member` (non-blank id). Label catalog += 4 `form_field_type` rows + a `visibility_op` domain (both locales).
  - **B. Prisma + migration (`20260713000000_form_builder_advanced`).** `enum FormFieldType` += `radio|checkbox|member|searchable` (`ALTER TYPE ‚Ä¶ ADD VALUE IF NOT EXISTS` ‚Äî purely additive, no rewrite). `form_fields` += nullable `visibility Json?` (ADD COLUMN ‚Äî the `form_fields_isolation` RLS policy is untouched; NULL = always-shown, no backfill / no data loss).
  - **C. API (`apps/api/src/forms/`).** `forms.dto.ts`: `FieldInputDto.key` is now OPTIONAL (server derives), + inline `options`/`optionStyle`/`allowOther` + `visibility` (nested `FieldVisibilityDto`/`VisibilityRuleDto`, `value` whitelisted via `@Allow()`). `forms.service.ts` `replaceFields` resolves each field's key (explicit kept stable; keyless ‚Üí `slugifyFieldKey` collision-suffixed), validates `validateVisibilityRefs` (rejects cycles/unknown refs **before** any write), upserts inline option sets via a new in-tx `upsertInlineOptionSet`, and persists `visibility`; `cloneDefinition` copies `visibility`. `forms-mapper.ts` returns `visibility`. Locked-core protection, non-destructive versioning, and `@@unique([formDefinitionId, key])` all preserved.
  - **D. Web.** `apps/web/app/forms/page.tsx` ‚Äî a label-first `<FieldEditor>` (no machine key shown), human type picker (`FORM_FIELD_TYPES`), inline choice rows (admin types choice LABELS; value auto-slugged) + "Allow Other" toggle, and a Pro conditional-logic editor ("Show this field only when ‚Ä¶ [field] [op] [value]", add-rule, all/any; refs limited to already-keyed fields). `apps/web/app/census/census-form.tsx` (the canonical multi-step renderer) now evaluates `visibleFields` live (cascades hide downstream fields, drop their answers, exclude from required-checks) and renders the four new types (`member`‚Üí`<MemberPicker>`, `searchable`‚Üí`<SearchSelect>`, `radio`‚Üíbutton group, `checkbox`/`multiselect`‚Üíchecklist). Prize/welfare/sharia keep their fixed surfaces but inherit the shared server-side evaluator + new-type validation.
  - **Acceptance (spec ¬ß5):** (1) admin builds typing labels only; keys auto-derive + stay unique; locked-core keys immutable ‚úÖ. (2) inline options create/update the OptionSet transparently; Other toggle works ‚úÖ. (3) radio/checkbox/member/searchable render + store; member‚Üíid; searchable typeaheads ‚úÖ. (4) conditional logic shows/hides live; multi-level cascades resolve; hidden field not required + ignored server-side; cycles rejected ‚úÖ. (5) web render + server validation share ONE evaluator ‚úÖ. (6) migration regression: enum extended, no data loss, RLS preserved, isolation absolute ‚úÖ. (7) gates green incl. isolation + i18n + web-coverage ‚úÖ.
  - **Decision noted:** the spec floated "`forbidNonWhitelisted` rejects a client-set key". Chosen instead: `key` is OPTIONAL on the DTO (server always derives for keyless fields; an explicit key is honored only to keep an EXISTING field's key stable so its option-set/visibility refs don't break on relabel). This satisfies acceptance #1 (admin never sees/types keys; keys auto-derive + stay unique; locked-core immutable) while keeping refs and the `@@unique` contract intact. New-field references in a condition require saving the draft once (a brand-new field has no stable key yet) ‚Äî surfaced as a builder hint, not an error.
  - **Gates:** typecheck ‚úÖ (shared/api/web), lint ‚úÖ (api, no warnings), web build ‚úÖ (all routes), API tests **1285/1285** ‚úÖ (i18n en‚áîur parity + web-coverage green ‚Äî `form_field_type` sweep now covers the 4 new types in both locales). NEW specs: `forms-helpers.spec.ts` (slugify, evaluate/visibleFields cascade, validateVisibilityRefs cycle/ref, validateSubmission honours visibility + new types), `forms.service.spec.ts` (auto-slug uniqueness, inline option upsert, visibility persist, cycle reject), NEW `form-builder-advanced.migration.spec.ts` (enum/column/RLS/isolation on the real migration chain). Zero physical-direction Tailwind; no new i18n `t()` keys (builder uses existing literal/`formatLabel` pattern). **Isolation ‚úÖ (enum + field-meta on the RLS-FORCEd form-builder tables).**

- **Build-step 64 ‚Äî Family-Tree Fix (marriage lens + two-lineage no-doubling)** üü¢ **complete ‚Äî `[CHECKPOINT]` (continuous mode).** branch `feat/64-family-tree-fix-v31` (off the staging head after 63); **WORK-TYPE: FIX** (corrects the shipped build-step-45 family tree). spec `specs/64-family-tree-fix-v31.md`, CODEREF `specs/61-64-CODEREF.md`. tests **1262/1262** (157 suites; **+6** net ‚Äî all in `family-tree.spec.ts`). **Wave 2 / item 4 ‚Äî closes Wave 2 (61‚Äì64).** **Tenant isolation ‚ûñ (not required) ‚Äî read-path/render fix ONLY: NO schema/Prisma/migration/RLS/`tenant_id`/permission-key/auth/endpoint/module change; `getFamily` still runs inside `runWithTenant` (RLS unchanged) and the de-dupe is a pure post-process on already-tenant-scoped data.**
  - **The two defects fixed (C-family-tree):** (1) under the **By-Marriage lens** the couple's **children** did not render (children were shown under `birth`/`both` only), so the marriage lens showed the spouse but never the family unit; (2) **two-lineage doubling** ‚Äî a member reached through BOTH lineages (a cousin marriage: a spouse who is also a blood relative) could render as TWO cards.
  - **A. Shared (`packages/shared/src/index.ts`).** Pure helpers (one source of truth for API + web + tests): `childVisibleUnderLens(lens, hasSpouseLink)` ‚Äî a child is a BIRTH relation so it always shows under `birth`/`both`; under `marriage` it shows ONLY when the other parent is present (`hasSpouseLink`), so the child renders beneath the couple. NEW `dedupeFamilyTree(view): FamilyTreeView` ‚Äî keeps the focal (the pivot) always, then drops from every other band any ref whose id was already placed in a higher-priority band (source order: ancestors father‚Üímother‚Üígrandparents ‚Üí spouses ‚Üí siblings ‚Üí children), so an overlapping member keeps its most-structural placement and the **marriage slot wins over siblings/children** (preserves the end-marriage affordance + Married-In chip). Pure + idempotent. `FamilyTreeView` shape UNCHANGED (band layout preserved ‚Äî no view-shape break).
  - **B. API (`apps/api/src/members/family.service.ts`).** `getFamily` builds the band view exactly as before (spouse slot already OPEN-SPOUSE_OF-only from build-step 61 ‚Äî divorced links never show under the live lens) then `return dedupeFamilyTree(view)` ‚Äî the API now returns a de-duped view so a two-lineage member surfaces ONCE. The "other parent" for children is the focal's open spouse, already resolved in `spouses` (so the web renders children under the couple without any new view field). `runWithTenant`/RLS, `toMemberRef`/`MemberRef`, the household overlay (`loadTreeHouseholds`), the paternal/maternal pivot, and the `husbandFacts` attached-fact node all untouched.
  - **C. Web (`apps/web/app/members/family-tree.tsx`).** Renamed the prop to `rawTree` and `const tree = useMemo(() => dedupeFamilyTree(rawTree), [rawTree])` ‚Äî de-dupes by member id at layout (idempotent belt-and-braces over the API; guards stale/partial data) so **no card renders twice**. Children band now gated by `showChildren = childVisibleUnderLens(lens, hasSpouseLink) && tree.children.length > 0`, where `hasSpouseLink = tree.spouses.length > 0 || tree.husbandFacts != null` ‚Äî so By-Marriage now shows the focal + open spouse(s) + their children as a unit (incl. when the other parent is the attached non-Okhai-husband fact); By-Birth = bloodline; By-Both = all (build-step-45 chips). Modal/focused view, household overlay + legend, click-to-refocus, RTL all preserved. **No new i18n keys** (reuses existing `members.*`/`genChildren`), so no dual-write needed.
  - **D. Tests (`apps/api/src/members/family-tree.spec.ts`, +6).** `childVisibleUnderLens` ‚Äî always-children under birth/both; marriage shows children only with a spouse link. `dedupeFamilyTree` ‚Äî a member that is BOTH an open spouse AND a blood sibling is kept once (in the marriage slot, dropped from siblings); focal never dropped + non-overlapping bands intact; idempotent. `FamilyService.getFamily` end-to-end ‚Äî a fake-tx focal with SPOUSE_OF + SIBLING_OF to the SAME member returns the cousin once (in `spouses`, `siblings` empty), proving the wiring. The build-step-45 lens-classifier + household-overlay tests stay green.
  - **Acceptance:** (1) By-Marriage shows the focal's open marriage(s) WITH the couple's children beneath; By-Birth bloodline; By-Both all ‚úÖ. (2) a two-lineage member renders exactly once ‚úÖ. (3) a divorced (closed) marriage stays out of the open lens (build-step 61) ‚Äî unchanged ‚úÖ. (4) build-step-45 behaviours (modal tree, household overlay, refocus, RTL, human labels) intact ‚úÖ. (5) gates green + family-tree spec extended ‚úÖ.
  - **Gates:** typecheck (all workspaces) ‚úÖ + web build ‚úÖ + lint ‚úÖ (api eslint + web next-lint, no warnings) + api tests **1262/1262** ‚úÖ + i18n parity + web-coverage GREEN (no new keys) + zero physical-direction Tailwind (RTL-safe). Shared rebuilt (`dist/`). Isolation ‚ûñ (read-path only ‚Äî reason above).
  - **Do-not-break kept:** `getFamily` tenant scoping (`runWithTenant`/RLS); `toMemberRef`/`MemberRef`; the household overlay (`loadTreeHouseholds`, build-step 45); the `husbandFacts` attached-fact node (the non-Okhai husband stays a fact, never a member node); the paternal/maternal pivot; the build-step-61 open-link rule.

- **Build-step 63 ‚Äî Card System (OMJ / Khundi / OMYS) + Certificate-Card Canvas** üü¢ **complete ‚Äî `[CHECKPOINT]` (continuous mode).** branch `feat/63-member-cards-canvas-v31` (off `feat/62` head ‚Äî 62 committed first as `ea5b831`); **WORK-TYPE: FEATURE** (extends the build-step-29/30 card + certificate system with two new member identifiers + per-placeholder/field styling). spec `specs/63-member-cards-canvas-v31.md`, CODEREF `specs/61-64-CODEREF.md`. tests **1256/1256** (157 suites; **+13** net). **Tenant isolation ‚úÖ** ‚Äî two `members` ADD COLUMNs; new migration regression proves columns added nullable, members RLS preserved (ENABLE+FORCE), OMJ unique kept / Khundi+OMYS NOT unique, and the new numbers are tenant-isolated (foreign tenant cannot read/write).
  - **A. Data model ‚Äî `members.khundiCardNumber` + `members.omysNumber` (migration `20260712000000_member_card_numbers`).** Two nullable `TEXT` columns (`khundi_card_number`, `omys_number`) added to `members` ‚Äî OPTIONAL secondary identifiers (Khundi-local card # + Okhai Memon Youth Services #). `omj_card_number` stays the canonical identity + its `(tenant_id, omj_card_number)` unique key; the two new columns carry **NO unique constraint** by default (a Khundi can reuse a number across members; per-tenant uniqueness is a future partial-unique if wanted). Pure ADD COLUMN ‚Äî `members_isolation` RLS untouched. **Styling adds NO columns** ‚Äî it extends the EXISTING JSON shapes (`CertificateTemplate.placeholders` + `CardTemplate.layout`). `schema.prisma` + `prisma generate` regenerated the client.
  - **B. Shared (`packages/shared/src/index.ts`).** NEW pure `clampHexColor(v, fallback?)` (`#rgb`/`#rrggbb`‚Üílowercase, else fallback/undefined) + `clampFontSize(v, fallback?)` (rounds, bounds to 4‚Äì400). `CertificatePlaceholder` gains optional `color?` (font/size/align already existed) ‚Äî `normalizeCertificatePlaceholders` now clamps font(trim+slice)/size(clampFontSize)/color(clampHexColor), back-compat (missing ‚Üí undefined ‚Üí renderer default). `CardLayoutField` gains optional `font?`/`size?`/`color?`; `CardLayout` gains `backgroundRef: string|null`; `DEFAULT_CARD_LAYOUT.backgroundRef = null`; `normalizeCardLayout` attaches per-field styling ONLY when valid (legacy `{key,label,show}` fields round-trip byte-identical ‚Üí `normalizeCardLayout({})` still `toEqual(DEFAULT_CARD_LAYOUT)`) + clamps `backgroundRef`. `MemberView` gains `khundiCardNumber`/`omysNumber`; `CardView` gains `memberKhundiCardNumber`/`memberOmysNumber` (read-through). **`buildCardQrPayload` UNCHANGED ‚Äî QR still encodes OMJ card # + ids ONLY, never a CNIC; `qrPayloadHasNoCnic` stays green (Khundi/OMYS deliberately NOT added to the QR).**
  - **C. API.** `members.dto.ts`: `CreateMemberDto`/`UpdateMemberDto` accept `khundiCardNumber?`/`omysNumber?` (`@IsString @MaxLength(64)`; free-form per-Khundi identifiers, trimmed in the service ‚Äî no canonical OMJ shape forced). `members.service.ts` create/update write the two columns (trim‚Üínull). `member-mapper.ts` `toMemberView` returns them. `vault-mapper.ts` `toCardView` + the 3 vault-service card `member` selects + the member-portal wallet card mappers (`toWalletCardView` + the synthesized default card + its 2 selects + `CardWithRelations`) now read-through `khundiCardNumber`/`omysNumber`. Certificate/card template SERVICES are unchanged in shape ‚Äî they already route writes through `normalizeCertificatePlaceholders` / `normalizeCardLayout`, so the extended styling validates automatically. `controllerNotes` (build-step 62) STILL never enters `MemberView`/portal/exports (re-asserted by a test).
  - **D. Web.** `members/member-form.tsx`: NEW optional **Khundi card #** + **OMYS #** inputs in the Pro profile-details section (OMJ stays the always-shown canonical identity); threaded through `FormState`/`initialState`/payload. `members/page.tsx`: NEW `<MemberInfoBoxes>` dashboard-style tiles (OMJ / Khundi / OMYS card numbers + status / age / household standing) rendered on the member-detail (tree) modal. `prize/certificate-canvas.tsx`: the selected-placeholder editor gains **font (preset family) / size / color** controls (align already present); canvas preview + `printCertificates` now apply `color` (+ existing font/size). `documents/card-visual.tsx`: `<CardVisual>` renders an optional **background image** (overrides the gradient) + applies per-field font/size/color to the name + card-number lines; `printCards` mirrors it. `documents/page.tsx` `TemplateDesigner`: NEW background `<ImageUpload>` (scope `certificate` ‚Äî reuses the existing template-art bucket; no new storage scope) + per-field (name / card-number) font/size/color controls; live preview. Reuses build-step-39 `<ImageUpload>`; zero physical-direction Tailwind (RTL-safe).

(Each section ALSO gates internally via `useEffectiveAccess` + `<AccessRequired>`, so this is defence-in-depth, not the only gate.)

(1) a TENANT admin holding `roles.manage` @ OWN_TENANT ‚Üí `assignmentsGrant(...)` = `true` (mode never reaches authz, so a Simple-mode user still passes); (2) a user without `roles.manage` ‚Üí `false` (Pro mode can't unlock it); (3) **`assignmentsGrant.length === 6`** ‚Äî the resolver signature has NO `mode` parameter, so mode *structurally cannot* gate a capability. - **Build-step 59 ‚Äî Modal submit shortcut + keyboard/ESC scoping** üü¢ **complete ‚Äî `[CHECKPOINT]` (continuous mode; presentation/keyboard only, NO schema/Prisma/migration/RLS/`tenant_id`/auth/permission-key/endpoint/module change).** branch `feat/59-modal-keyboard-v31` (off `staging` head after 58); **WORK-TYPE: FIX** (completes the build-step-39 `<Modal>` primitive ‚Äî spec header declares FIX; branch keeps the spec's `feat/59-‚Ä¶` name). spec `specs/59-modal-keyboard-v31.md`, CODEREF `specs/54-60-CODEREF.md`. tests **1213/1213** (149 suites; no new api test ‚Äî the change is web React with no web test harness, matching the build-step-58 precedent where only the shared pure logic was unit-tested; correctness covered by typecheck+build+the existing suite). **Tenant isolation ‚ûñ** (keyboard/overlay behaviour only; no data access path touched).
  - **NEW `apps/web/app/lib/hotkeys.ts` (the rush-time substrate, reused by build-step 72 attendance roll-call):** `useHotkeys(map, opts)` binds combo‚Üíhandler on a target (default `window`), cleans up on unmount, and skips a bare single-key combo while the user is typing in an input/textarea/contenteditable UNLESS a command modifier is held (so type-to-find + single-key toggles coexist). Pure, DOM-light, exported helpers: `parseHotkey` (`'mod+enter'`‚Üítokens; `mod` = Cmd OR Ctrl; aliases esc/enter/space/arrows/del), `matchesHotkey(combo, eventLike)`, `hasCommandModifier`, `isTypingTarget`. `useEscapeDismiss(active, onEscape)` ‚Äî the ESC-scoping helper for custom dropdowns.
  - **`<Modal>`/`<Drawer>` (`ui/modal.tsx`): opt-in `onSubmitShortcut?: () => void`.** Threaded through `OverlayShell` ‚Üí `useFocusTrap`; the existing capture-phase keydown handler now fires it on `Enter` **with** `metaKey||ctrlKey` (preventDefault+stopPropagation), so Cmd/Ctrl+Enter saves while **plain** Enter is never intercepted (textarea newlines + native form submit intact). Held in a ref so a fresh handler each render doesn't re-bind the trap (no focus-restore thrash). Build-step-39 ESC/focus-trap/Tab-wrap/scroll-lock/`dismissible`/drawer-slide all unchanged.
  - **ESC scoping (the core fix, C19):** `<SearchSelect>`/`<MultiSearchSelect>` (`search-select.tsx` `useDismiss`), `<MemberPicker>`, `<DateField>`, and `<ColumnsControl>` now close their own popover via `useEscapeDismiss` ‚Äî a **window**-CAPTURE keydown listener that calls `stopPropagation()` + closes. Rationale (documented in `hotkeys.ts`): the modal traps ESC with a **document**-CAPTURE listener; the capture phase walks `window ‚Üí document ‚Üí ‚Ä¶ ‚Üí target`, so a window-capture listener fires BEFORE the modal's document-capture one and stops the event from ever reaching it. Result: ESC with a dropdown open closes only the dropdown (modal stays); a second ESC (dropdown gone, its listener removed) reaches the modal and closes it. (Replaces the document-bubble `stopPropagation` columns-control shipped in 55, which couldn't actually preempt a document-capture listener.) Outside-click `mousedown` handlers left on `document` as before.

PURE helpers: `isActiveFilterValue`, `activeFilterCount`, `normalizeForMatch` (lowercase/trim/collapse-ws), `applyFilters(rows, config, state, accessor)` (AND across active fields; fuzzy text = normalized substring; select exact; multiselect membership; boolean true/false; numberRange + dateRange inclusive bounds; ISO dates compared on the date part so a `‚Ä¶THH:mm` value still falls inside a `yyyy-mm-dd` bound), `filtersToQuery(state)` / `queryToFilters(query, config)` (round-trip serialization: string‚Üí`field`, array‚Üí`field=v1,v2`, boolean‚Üí`field=true|false`, range‚Üí`field_min`/`field_max`, date‚Üí`field_from`/`field_to`; empty/inactive omitted), `shouldFilterServerSide(config, total)` (`total > cap`).

Internal `filterState`; `serverSide = shouldFilterServerSide(config, totalRowCount ?? rows.length)`. Client path applies `applyFilters` inside the existing `filtered` memo (after the free-text search, so they compose); server path fires a guarded effect (callback held in a ref; keyed on the serialized query) that calls `onServerFilter`. Export still exports the FILTERED set. A list with no `filterConfig` behaves exactly as before.

- **(history) build-step 46 ‚Äî Storage rework: Google Drive backend + per-Khundi quota + auto-compression** ‚úÖ **complete ‚Äî `[FIXED_CHECKPOINT]` (hard; changes the file-storage backend + adds a new tenant-DATA table + quota enforcement ‚Üí manual approve)** ‚Äî branch `feat/46-storage-drive-quota` (off `feat/45-family-tree`); **WORK-TYPE: FEATURE** (Drive backend + quota + compression are NEW capability; extends `StorageService` = the FIX half); spec `specs/46-storage-drive-quota.md`, CODEREF `specs/43-53-CODEREF.md`. **DATA-MODEL CHANGE (migration `20260703000000_storage_quota_v2`, additive/non-destructive):** NEW tenant-DATA table **`storage_objects`** (the scope-agnostic usage LEDGER ‚Äî one row per stored object across every upload scope; `ENABLE+FORCE` RLS `app_rls_bypass() OR tenant_id=app_current_tenant_id()`, UNIQUE `(tenant_id, storage_key)`, FK‚Üítenants CASCADE), plus nullable `tenants.storage_quota_mb` (per-Khundi cap override; NULL‚Üídefault) + nullable `documents.original_size` (pre-compression bytes). **NO new permission-key / NO auth change** ‚Äî reuses `settings.manage`@OWN_TENANT (tenant cap), `crossKhundi.view`@ALL_TENANTS (OMJ read) + `tenant.manage`@PLATFORM (OMJ cap write). **The `StorageService` CONTRACT is stable** (presign/publicUrl unchanged for R2) so the step-39 `<FileUpload>` + step-30 doc refs are untouched. **Five parts:** **(1) ENV-selectable backend** ‚Äî NEW `backends.ts`: `StorageBackend` interface + `R2Backend` (existing presign logic extracted, behaviour-identical), `GoogleDriveBackend` (service-account JWT via `node:crypto` RS256 + Drive REST via fetch, one folder per Khundi, uploads/downloads PROXIED through the API since Drive has no S3 presign), `DevBackend` (placeholder URLs), `createStorageBackend(read)` selects by `STORAGE_BACKEND` (`r2`|`gdrive`|`dev`; default r2; unknown‚Üír2). Every backend DEV-falls-back when its creds are unset (parity with R2's existing posture). `.env.example` gains `STORAGE_BACKEND` + `GDRIVE_CLIENT_EMAIL`/`GDRIVE_PRIVATE_KEY`/`GDRIVE_ROOT_FOLDER_ID`. **(2) Per-Khundi quota** ‚Äî NEW `StorageQuotaService` (RLS-scoped): used-bytes = `SUM(storage_objects.byteSize)` (computed ‚Üí no running-total drift; a delete removes the row), cap = `tenants.storage_quota_mb ?? DEFAULT_STORAGE_QUOTA_MB` (500). `recordObject` is idempotent on the key + does the quota check + write in ONE transaction on the DELTA (a replace never counts an object's old size against itself); `assertWithinQuota` enforces on presign (declared size, UX) + commit (stored size, authoritative); `removeObject` reclaims on delete. NEW shared (`@kc/shared`): `DEFAULT_STORAGE_QUOTA_MB`, `MB`, `MAX_UPLOAD_BYTES`, `mbToBytes`/`bytesToMb`/`effectiveQuotaMb`/`wouldExceedQuota`, `storageUsageView`, `StorageBackendKind`, `StorageUsageView`, `TenantStorageUsage`. **(3) Auto-compression** ‚Äî server owns the POLICY (`compressionPlanFor` ‚Üí processable JPEG/PNG/WebP re-encode to WebP, cap 1600px, q0.82; SVG/GIF/PDF/non-images stored as-is) + the GUARD (`MAX_UPLOAD_BYTES`) + the ACCOUNTING (`original_size` vs stored `byteSize`); because the upload is presigned DIRECT-to-storage (and the build env has no native image codec), the actual re-encode runs CLIENT-side in `<FileUpload>` via `<canvas>` (downscale + re-encode, only kept if smaller), reporting the post-compression size to the server ‚Äî documented split, the same `compressionPlanFor` policy can drive a future server-side codec on the proxied Drive path without a contract change. **(4) Surfaces** ‚Äî `POST /storage/commit` (record stored size, idempotent), `GET /storage/usage`, `PATCH /storage/quota` (`settings.manage`, audited), `DELETE /storage/object` (reclaim), the Drive `PUT|GET /storage/proxy` byte-proxy (key re-checked in-tenant), + NEW `StoragePlatformController` (`GET /platform/storage/usage` `crossKhundi.view`@ALL_TENANTS, `PATCH /platform/storage/:tenantId/quota` `tenant.manage`@PLATFORM, both `runAsPlatform`). **Web:** Settings ‚Üí Storage tab is now a real `<StorageSection>` (used/total bar, backend label, compression note, admin cap setter); the OMJ "Tenants & Modules" page gains a `<StorageCaps>` panel (per-Khundi usage + cap set); `<FileUpload>`/`<ImageUpload>` optimize‚Üícommit‚Üíreclaim (over-quota 403 ‚Üí `StorageQuotaError` hint, blob reclaimed). The vault's document create/delete now record/decrement the ledger (server-side, the canonical decrement). Storage plumbing paths (`storage/upload-url`, `storage/commit`, `storage/proxy`) added to `AUDIT_SUPPRESSED_PATHS` (high-frequency churn; the meaningful `documents.upload` + `storage.set_quota` stay audited). **(5) Proof** ‚Äî Gates: typecheck ‚úÖ (shared/api/web 6/6), lint ‚úÖ (web + api, no warnings), web build ‚úÖ (all 33 routes; `/settings` 11.9 kB, `/platform/tenants` 4.42 kB), tests **1076/1076** ‚úÖ (1057 + 19 NEW: `storage.isolation.spec.ts` √ó8 ‚Äî RLS read/insert-WITH-CHECK/delete isolation on `storage_objects`, per-Khundi SUM, replace-by-DELTA no-double-count, cap invisible cross-tenant, platform grouped usage; `storage-policy.spec.ts` √ó11 ‚Äî compression plan processable/as-is, quota math + boundary, usage view, backend selection + DEV fallback + live R2 presign + Drive proxy). i18n: en‚áîur parity + web-coverage gates GREEN (NEW `settings.storage*`/`upload.overQuota`+`optimizing`/`platform.storage*` keys authored in BOTH locales in `messages-extra.ts` + `i18n-deltas/{common-ui,platform}.json`). a refused delete is a 409, never this shape. **9 NEW tenant-scoped DELETE endpoints with the spec-42 decision rule + referential/immutability guards:** (1) **welfare case type** ‚Äî hard-delete if unused, else ARCHIVE (`active=false`, kept for case history); (2) **welfare case** ‚Äî hard-delete a pre-disbursement case, REFUSE (409) once ANY disbursement exists (disbursed welfare facts are immutable ‚Äî reverse in accounting, never erase); (3) **prize ceremony** ‚Äî hard-delete a draft/empty one, REFUSE if it has applications; (4) **prize category** ‚Äî hard-delete if unused, else ARCHIVE; (5) **prize gift** ‚Äî always a clean hard-delete (assignments copy the label as free text, no FK); (6) **prize certificate template** ‚Äî hard-delete if unused, REFUSE while a ceremony links it; (7) **event** ‚Äî hard-delete a draft/scheduled one with no RSVPs, REFUSE a completed event or one with RSVP/attendance (archive instead); recorded spend stays in accounting regardless (no event FK); (8) **census snapshot** ‚Äî hard-delete only an empty, still-open round, REFUSE a finalized one or one with submissions; (9) **document** ‚Äî hard-delete the metadata row (non-financial; blob lifecycle owned by ¬ß46). **EDIT (reuses the step-39 create modals, pre-filled, permission-gated):** events (PATCH), welfare cases (PATCH, pre-disbursement fields only ‚Äî backend already restricts to open/under-inquiry), prize ceremonies (PATCH), notification templates (PUT, edit-in-place author form). Members already shipped full edit+delete (build-step 39); notification-template delete already existed (build-step 33). **NEW shared `<ConfirmDialog>` (`apps/web/app/ui/confirm-dialog.tsx`)** ‚Äî built on `<Modal>` (focus-trap/ESC/scroll-lock/RTL), `danger` confirm by default, non-dismissible while busy; every destructive action routes through it (no single-click delete) and every trigger is `hasPermission`-gated (a user who can't edit/delete never sees the control). **IMMUTABILITY BOUNDARY pinned (`apps/api/src/audit/edit-delete-immutability.spec.ts`):** asserts `AccountingService` exposes NO `delete*`/`remove*` and no posted-entry update (corrections are reversing entries, ¬ß18), and `AuditService` is append-only (no delete/update on the recorder) ‚Äî so a future regression that adds a delete to accounting/audit fails loudly. Gates: typecheck ‚úÖ (shared/api/web), lint ‚úÖ (web + api, no warnings), tests **1026/1026** ‚úÖ (1002 + 24: welfare-delete √ó5, prize-delete √ó5, events-delete √ó4, census-delete √ó4, vault-delete √ó2, immutability-boundary √ó4), build ‚úÖ (all 30 routes; `/welfare` 11.5 kB, `/prize` 12 kB, `/events` 6.66 kB, `/census` 20.5 kB, `/documents` 8.68 kB). i18n: en‚áîur parity + web-coverage gates GREEN (new edit/delete copy added in both locales ‚Äî `common.*` edit/delete/archive/confirm/save + per-module delete confirms). **NOTE:** no live DB/staging in the build env ‚Äî RLS + immutability proven on PGlite/unit fakes; the operator runs the staging deploy + live screenshots (edit modal pre-filled, delete confirm dialog, an archived case type, an attempted delete of a disbursed case ‚Üí blocked, a permission-gated control hidden) per the spec before promotion. **‚úÖ `[FIXED_CHECKPOINT]` ‚Äî APPROVED (operator instruction, 2026-06-25).** ‚è≠Ô∏è NEXT: build-step 43 ‚Äî Settings consolidation + Role editor UI (spec `specs/43-settings-roles.md`).

- **Last session summary (build-step 20 ‚Äî Shared Form-Builder engine):** Branched `feature/20-form-builder` off `staging`. Built build-step 20 per `specs/20-form-builder.md` ‚Äî the reusable, per-Khundi, **versioned form-definition engine** that powers Census (build-step 24) + Prize (build-step 29) (ARCHITECTURE ¬ß32). **WORK-TYPE: FEATURE** (new cross-cutting subsystem). **Prisma:** 3 new TENANT-DATA tables ‚Äî `form_definitions` (`purpose` census/prize, `version`, `label`, `is_default`, `status` draft/active/archived, `created_by`; unique `(tenant,purpose,version)`), `form_fields` (`key`, `label`, `type` text/number/date/select/multiselect/boolean/file, `is_locked_core`, `required`, `order`, `step_index`, `option_set_id` [soft ref, no FK], `validation` JSON, `help_text`; unique `key` per definition) and `option_sets` (`field_key`, `style` light/detailed, `options` JSON `{value,label}`, `allow_other`) + enums `FormPurpose`/`FormFieldType`/`FormDefinitionStatus`/`OptionSetStyle` ‚Äî hand-authored migration `20260620000000_form_builder`; **all three carry the ¬ß-template RLS** (ENABLE+FORCE, `*_isolation` policies reusing the step-2 helpers). Field cascades from definition; all three cascade from tenant. **The engine stores DEFINITIONS ONLY ‚Äî the consuming module owns the answers** (census_entries.data / prize payloads) and calls the engine's validator before writing. **`@kc/shared`:** the form contract as PURE FUNCTIONS + types ‚Äî the `LOCKED_CORE` registry (census: household/relation_to_head/name/gender/dob/marital_status/is_okhai_by_birth/omj_card/education/profession/disability; **income_band deliberately OPTIONAL, not locked-core**; prize: applicant/category/criterion/supporting_doc), `lockedCoreKeys`/`isLockedCoreKey`/`missingLockedCoreKeys` (locked-core protection), `validateSubmission` (required / number range / text maxLen+regex / option-set membership incl. allow-Other / unconstrained-when-no-set), `coreAnswersOnly` (the ¬ß7.5 cross-Khundi rule ‚Äî custom fields dropped from Jamat aggregation by construction; OMJ still sees all per-Khundi), `formStepLayout` (multi-step render schema), the default ladders (`DEFAULT_INCOME_OPTIONS_LIGHT` Below/Average/Above; `DEFAULT_INCOME_OPTIONS_DETAILED` **PKR Below 40,000 / 40,001‚Äì80,000 / 80,001‚Äì150,000 / 150,001‚Äì250,000 / 250,000+** [`[DECIDE AT BUILD]` ‚Üí adopted, recorded in decisions table]; `DEFAULT_EDUCATION_OPTIONS`; `DEFAULT_PROFESSION_OPTIONS`), + the `FormDefinitionView`/`FormFieldView`/`OptionSetView`/`FormStep`/`OptionItem`/`FormFieldValidation` types + catalogs. **NEW permission `forms.manage`** (CORE module ‚Äî the engine is cross-cutting infrastructure, NOT a sellable module, so no module-flag gate; OWN_TENANT) ‚Äî added to Khundi Super Admin (auto via SUPER_ADMIN_KEYS), President + General Secretary default roles; NOT in NON_TENANT_KEYS. **NestJS `FormsModule`:** `FormsService` (all on `runWithTenant` RLS path) ‚Äî listDefinitions/getDefinition/**getActiveDefinition** (the read contract exported for census/prize), provisionDefault (default-then-customize, **idempotent** ‚Äî builds the default option sets + an active default definition via the shared `defaultFormSpec`), cloneDefinition (new DRAFT version copying fields ‚Äî prior answers untouched), updateDefinition (label/status; Deferred (noted in decisions): member self-apply/registration via the ¬ß22 PWA, PDF card printing + QR camera scanner UI, full per-request enforcement of the document `access_roles` row filter on reads (the field + `canViewDocument` helper + gate ship now). **Prior build-step 17 (now APPROVED):** **Build-step 17 essentials:** `audit_log` is the ¬ß7.11 immutable log ‚Äî TENANT DATA on the ¬ß-template RLS BUT **append-only** (only SELECT+INSERT policies, NO UPDATE/DELETE ‚Üí a row can never be edited/erased even by its owner tenant; proven by isolation + migration specs). `tenant_id` nullable (null = platform-level action) + SET NULL on tenant delete (trail survives detached). Rows are written by a GLOBAL `AuditInterceptor` (`APP_INTERCEPTOR`) on every successful POST/PUT/PATCH/DELETE ‚Äî **no per-module wiring** (existing module service specs untouched, all still green); it stores actor/action/target/tenant + a SAFE metadata subset (method/path/host/non-id params ‚Äî **NEVER the request body**, so no secret/CNIC/OTP is captured). `AuditService.record` is path-aware (tenant‚Üí`runWithTenant`, platform‚Üí`runAsPlatform`), re-sanitises metadata, and is NON-throwing (auditing can't break the audited action). New key `audit.view` (CORE): tenant `/audit` OWN_TENANT (President + Super Admin), cross-tenant `/platform/audit` ALL_TENANTS (OMJ Admin) / PLATFORM (Vendor). `sanitizeAuditMetadata` (shared, pure) redacts any value under a sensitive key (defense in depth). **i18n is now real, not just "RTL-ready":** `@kc/shared` `MESSAGES` EN/UR catalog + `translate` (en‚Üíkey fallback) + `isRtlLocale`/`dirForLocale`; web `app/i18n.tsx` `I18nProvider` flips `<html lang/dir>` at runtime (Urdu = full RTL, no reload) + `LanguageToggle`. Accessibility baseline in `globals.css` (focus-visible, skip link, large targets, reduced-motion, Nastaliq RTL face). The only API change is a **read-only** extension of `getPlatformDashboard` to also sum each tenant's (RLS-isolated) `subscriptions`+`payments` for ¬ß20 revenue, reusing the build-step-15 `toPaymentView`/`summarizeBilling`. New shared pure fns: `summarizePlatformRevenue` (never nets collected vs outstanding; reuses `summarizeBilling` per tenant) + `censusHeatBand` (5-band heatmap classifier). **Deferred (noted in decisions):** impersonation (`tenant.impersonate` ‚Äî auth-touching, a focused later step), graveyard-records view (Phase-2 `death_records`, build-step 18), a dedicated OMJ Jamat-AI-insights panel, PDF/Excel export. **Billing model:** `subscription_plans` is GLOBAL reference data (no RLS, like `permissions`); `subscriptions` + `payments` are tenant DATA (RLS, one subscription per tenant, plan FK RESTRICT, payment‚Üísubscription FK SET NULL). Money is whole-rupee Int (PKR). New keys `billing.view` (OWN_TENANT) + `billing.manage` (PLATFORM Vendor duty, in `NON_TENANT_KEYS`, ‚âÝ tenant.manage). **White-label adds NO column** ‚Äî branding is `tenants.branding` JSON + `tenants.custom_domain`; `effectiveBranding` APPLIES it ONLY when the `whitelabel` module flag is ON (else KhundiConnect defaults, retained-but-not-applied, ¬ß15.3); `GET /tenants/current` honours this. `sanitizeBranding` whitelists the ¬ß15.2 safe subset (logo/brandName/hex colors/tagline) ‚Äî re-sanitized on save. `/settings/branding` is module-gated (paid ‚Üí reachable; off ‚Üí 404 whole surface). Module-toggle UI (`/platform/tenants`) is the build-step 5 one (unchanged) ‚Äî build-step 15 added billing + branding around it. **Member portal `/me/*` is IDENTITY-gated, not permission-gated:** the service resolves the member from the AUTHENTICATED card (`user.omjCardNumber`) vs the resolved-host tenant on `runWithTenant`, so a card holder reaches only their OWN record (a non-member card ‚Üí 404); `@RequireModule('portal')` still gates it (default-open). The admin `/portal/*` queue is dual-gated (`portal.requests`/`portal.suggestions`). **¬ß22 SAFE-FIELD rule is structural:** `sanitizeProfileChanges` whitelists name/dob/education/occupation/income/contact and DROPS status/card/CNIC/member-type/gender ‚Äî a member can never self-edit a constitutional field; the set is re-sanitized again at approval time. A profile change is applied to the member ONLY on an explicit admin approve (¬ß3.5). The PWA service worker NEVER caches `/api/*` (member data + auth must stay fresh + session-scoped on a shared phone). Demo: sign in as `OMJ-JAF-0002` (OTP-only) on jafrani-b ‚Üí `/me`. **Reports add NO table/migration:** they DERIVE dashboards from members/lawazim/accounting/census via the SAME shared pure functions those modules use (one source of truth ‚Äî `MembersService.demographics` now also delegates to the shared `computeMemberDemographics`). The Khundi altitude reads on `runWithTenant` (RLS-isolated); the OMJ (`crossKhundi.view` ALL_TENANTS) + Vendor (`tenant.manage` PLATFORM) altitudes read on the audited `runAsPlatform` path and have NO per-tenant module gate (mirrors Vendor provisioning). The rich OMJ/Vendor dashboard UIs land with build-step 16; build-step 13 shipped the full Khundi dashboard UI + all three altitude APIs + CSV exports. After editing shared, rebuild `@kc/shared` before jest/typecheck/build (done). **AI generator SIMULATES insights unless `AI_LIVE=on`** and **messaging dispatcher SIMULATES sends unless `MESSAGING_LIVE=on`** (both optional env, default off) ‚Äî so dev/staging/seed/gates never hit a provider, send PII, or bill anyone; live wiring flips the env on with real per-owner keys. **AI privacy (¬ß11.6) is structural:** insights are built ONLY from anonymized aggregate counts (`aggregateMembersForInsight` drops names/CNIC) + `assertAnonymized` is a runtime backstop before any real provider call. **ai_insights RLS is a DELIBERATE widening** of the ¬ß-template ‚Äî a tenant reads its own KHUNDI rows PLUS shared JAMAT rows (`tenant_id IS NULL`), gated on a tenant context (no-context still sees nothing); writes are own-KHUNDI-only (JAMAT rows are bypass-path only). After editing the schema, **rebuild `@kc/shared` (`npm run build -w @kc/shared`) before running jest** ‚Äî jest maps `@kc/shared` to its SOURCE for tests, but typecheck/build resolve the built `dist/index.d.ts`, so rebuild shared before typecheck/build when you add shared exports. PGlite UUID literals must be **hex-only** (0-9a-f) ‚Äî `s`/`n` etc. are invalid. Gate infra notes: isolation + migration gates use **PGlite** (in-process Postgres/WASM, no Docker/superuser); jest needs `NODE_OPTIONS=--experimental-vm-modules` (wired into the api `test` script). Service tests use pure-function fixtures + a fake transaction client, so no live services are needed (the accounting fake must set `entryId` on nested-created journal lines so the include join resolves). After editing the schema run `npm run prisma:generate` from `apps/api` before typecheck/build (set a dummy `DATABASE_URL` for `prisma validate`/`generate`). **`nest build` gotcha: `incremental:true` + `deleteOutDir` means a leftover `*.tsbuildinfo` makes tsc skip emit after dist is wiped (exit 0, empty dist) ‚Äî `rm -f *.tsbuildinfo` before a clean build to verify; the turbo `npm run build` from root is the canonical build gate (it reported 3 successful).** NOTE: a stray `*/` inside a Prisma `///` doc comment will corrupt the generated client's `.d.ts` ‚Äî keep doc comments clean. NOTE: `prisma/*.ts` (seed/reset) is outside the `src/**` typecheck scope and runs via `ts-node --transpile-only`; type-check it manually after edits.

| 2026-06-06 | `audit_log` is append-only at the DB (immutable) | Per ¬ß7.11 "immutable", `audit_log` carries ENABLE+FORCE RLS with ONLY a SELECT policy + an INSERT policy ‚Äî no UPDATE/DELETE policy, so those commands match nothing and are denied even to the table-owner application role. A row, once written, can never be edited or erased. Proven by `audit.isolation.spec` (owner UPDATE/DELETE affects 0 rows) + `audit.migration.spec` (`pg_policies` shows only SELECT+INSERT). `reset.ts` clears it on the bypass path for dev re-seeding only. | confirm design |
| 2026-06-06 | `audit_log.tenant_id` is nullable + SET NULL on tenant delete | A platform-level action (Vendor provisioning, OMJ cross-tenant read) has no single Khundi, so `tenant_id` is null (the ¬ß-template policy `tenant_id = app_current_tenant_id()` excludes null rows from a tenant session ‚Äî a Khundi never sees platform-level audit; only the bypass path does). On tenant delete the FK SET NULLs so the trail SURVIVES (detached, platform-path-only) rather than being erased ‚Äî an immutable log shouldn't vanish with a tenant. | confirm design |
| 2026-06-06 | Audit is captured by a GLOBAL interceptor, not per-module hooks | `AuditInterceptor` (`APP_INTERCEPTOR`) records ONE row for every successful POST/PUT/PATCH/DELETE across EVERY module ‚Äî the ¬ß22 cross-cutting "audit hook" with NO per-module wiring (existing module services + their specs are untouched, all 521 still green). It stores actor/action(method+route)/target(`:id` or created id)/tenant + a SAFE metadata subset (method/path/host/non-id params) and **NEVER the request body**, so no credential/OTP/CNIC is captured (¬ß17). Richer per-action explicit `AuditService.record` calls are an incremental follow-on. | confirm design |

| 2026-06-06 | `sanitizeAuditMetadata` is the structural secrets guarantee | Any value under a sensitive key (password/pass/secret/token/otp/auth/credential/apiKey/api_key/key/cnic/cipher/encrypted ‚Äî substring, case-insensitive) ‚Üí `[redacted]`, recursively; strings/objects/arrays are length/depth/breadth-capped. | 2026-06-05 | AI generation simulates unless `AI_LIVE=on` | The `InsightGenerator` only makes a real OpenAI/Claude HTTP call when the optional `AI_LIVE` env = `on`; otherwise it SIMULATES (returns a deterministic offline insight from the same aggregate via `simulateInsight`, no network). | 2026-06-05 | AI privacy is structural (¬ß11.6) | Insights are built ONLY from `aggregateMembersForInsight` (counts, never names/CNIC) ‚Üí `buildInsightPrompt` references only the aggregate. `assertAnonymized` is a runtime backstop the generator calls before EVERY real provider request (throws on a CNIC/phone pattern). | 2026-06-05 | `ai_insights` RLS widened for cross-altitude visibility | Unlike the standard ¬ß-template, `ai_insights` READ = own KHUNDI rows OR shared JAMAT rows (`tenant_id IS NULL`) ‚Äî but the JAMAT clause requires a tenant context so a no-context session still sees nothing (deny-by-default). WRITE (FOR ALL) = own KHUNDI only; a tenant can never forge/modify a JAMAT row or a rival's (WITH CHECK). This implements ¬ß11.3 (Jamat insights shared downward, anonymized; never sideways). `ai_config` keeps the plain ¬ß-template (Khundi never sees OMJ's key). | confirm design |
| 2026-06-05 | AI Insights permission duty split | No new keys/module ‚Äî the catalog already has `insights.{view,generate}` + `ai_key.manage` + module `insights`. | 2026-06-05 | AI config = encrypted key + non-secret provider/model | The per-owner provider API key is stored as ONE AES-256-GCM ciphertext via the SAME `CnicCipherService` cipher, decrypted only in-memory at generate time, never returned (`AiConfigView.hasApiKey` only) or logged. `provider`/`model`/`enabled` are non-secret and shown in the UI. Mapped: `view`=read config + comm log, `send`=compose+send, `config`=set provider/sender/enabled, `messaging_key.manage`=set the SECRET provider credentials (separate, write-only ‚Äî mirrors `ai_key.manage`). Added `notifications.config` + `messaging_key.manage` to the **General Secretary** default role (the ¬ß9 "notifications" owner); Super Admin already holds all. | confirm mapping |
| 2026-06-05 | Provider credentials = encrypted JSON blob | The per-tenant Twilio/Infobip credentials are stored as ONE AES-256-GCM-encrypted JSON string (e.g. Twilio `{accountSid,authToken}` / Infobip `{apiKey,baseUrl}`) via the SAME `CnicCipherService` cipher, decrypted only in-memory at send time. Never returned (`MessagingConfigView.hasCredentials` only) or logged (¬ß17). `from_label` (sender id/number) is non-secret and shown in the UI. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Comm log recipients stored as JSON | `notifications.recipients` is a JSON array of `{memberId?, name?, phone}`; counts (`recipient_count`/`sent_count`/`failed_count`) + `status` are stored alongside for fast log reads. A member is never messaged twice in one send (`normalizeRecipients` dedups by phone). | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Seed records log rows, never sends | The seed writes per-tenant messaging config (encrypted demo credentials) + 4 historical comm-log rows directly (a record of past sends); it NEVER calls the dispatcher, so no message is ever sent during seeding. Demo credentials are non-functional and would be simulated anyway. | confirm (demo) |
| 2026-06-05 | One double-entry engine (no "simple" data model) | Per ¬ß18, EVERY transaction ‚Äî simple cashbook or detailed journal ‚Äî is stored as balanced `journal_lines`. `accounting_settings.mode` is a VIEW flag only; `setMode` upserts that row and never reads/rewrites journal data (proven non-destructive by `accounting.service.spec`). The engine refuses any unbalanced/both-sided/zero entry. | confirm reading |
| 2026-06-05 | Cash side = a default "Cash & Bank" asset account | The double-entry cash side uses a seeded `isDefault` ASSET head ("Cash & Bank"); a line may also carry `bank_account_id` to attribute the movement to a physical bank. The cashbook = the asset-line ledger (debit=in, credit=out); opening balance = Œ£ `bank_accounts.opening_balance`. Keeps simple-mode auto-assignment unambiguous. | confirm |
| 2026-06-05 | Default chart auto-provisioned (default-open) | A tenant's default chart of accounts is auto-created on first accounting access (idempotent) AND seeded explicitly for the demo tenants. Mirrors the build-step 5 "module default = open" stance ‚Äî a freshly-provisioned Khundi can use accounting immediately. Added an "OMJ Lawazim Remittance" expense head (beyond the ¬ß7.6 list) so the ¬ß2.5 bulk remittance posts to a clearly-separate head. | confirm (default-open + extra head) |
| 2026-06-05 | Accounting permission duty split | No new keys/module ‚Äî the catalog already has `accounting.{view,entry,mode,banks,reports}` + module `accounting`. Mapped: `view`=read books, `entry`=record (simple/detailed) + add custom heads, `mode`=switch simple/detailed, `banks`=manage bank accounts, `reports`=ledger/financial summary. Account-head creation maps to `entry`. | confirm mapping |
| 2026-06-05 | Lawazim‚Üíaccounting live auto-posting deferred | ¬ß18 describes lawazim posting income/remittance entries into accounting. To keep the build-step boundary clean and build-step 9 GREEN, LawazimService is left untouched (no live auto-post wired). The integration is DEMONSTRATED in the seed (this-year payments post as income, the OMJ remittance as a separate expense ‚Äî never netted, ¬ß2.5) and the shared posting maths exist; live wiring is a small follow-on. | confirm (defer live wiring) |
| 2026-06-05 | `journal_lines` carries `tenant_id` | Like `member_status_history`, the child `journal_lines` gets its own `tenant_id` + RLS for isolation parity (no tenant-DATA table without RLS), beyond reaching it via the parent entry. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Jafrani-B detailed, others simple (seed) | ¬ß31.3 asks for one tenant in each accounting mode; seeded Jafrani-B in DETAILED and Toberiya-A/Kath-A in SIMPLE so both interfaces are demoable on real data. Demo bank opening balance Rs 50000. | confirm (demo) |
| 2026-06-05 | Lawazim liability = voting eligibility | The ¬ß2.5 fee is "per 18+ male member". `isLawazimLiable` DELEGATES to `isVotingEligible` (active ‚àß male ‚àß 18+ ‚àß memberType=member) so the fee population and the constitutional voting population can never drift apart; named separately so a future divergence (e.g. should an honorary ever owe) is a one-line change. Derived on read, never stored. | confirm reading |
| 2026-06-05 | Two independent ledgers, no money movement | The Khundi fee (income, `lawazim_payments`) and the OMJ fee (expense, `omj_remittances`) are SEPARATE. `summarizeLawazimYear` computes `collected` and `omj.remitted` from disjoint inputs and NEVER nets one against the other; the service records each independently. This is the ¬ß2.5 "NO AUTO-DEDUCTION / NO AUTO-TRANSFER" rule, asserted by `lawazim.service.spec`. | confirm reading |
| 2026-06-05 | Khundi fee Rs 1500 / OMJ fee Rs 100 (seed) | Seeded the ¬ß2.5 example figures (Jafrani-B Khundi fee Rs 1500/yr; OMJ fee the fixed Rs 100/yr default). Real per-tenant fees are set via the UI; these are demo values only. | confirm (demo figures) |
| 2026-06-05 | Amounts stored as whole-rupee Int | PKR fees/payments/remittances are stored as integer rupees (no decimals/paisa) ‚Äî matches the ¬ß2.5 examples, avoids float rounding, keeps the cashbook exact. | confirm |
| 2026-06-05 | Partial payments allowed; status derived | A member may have many payments per year; standing (paid/partial/unpaid) is DERIVED by summing them vs the Khundi fee ‚Äî no stored "paid" flag. Over-payment still reads `paid`; a since-removed member's payment is retained (SET NULL) and counts as income but not against any member's debt. | confirm |
| 2026-06-05 | Fee-config set = `lawazim.record` | Setting the per-year fee config is mapped to the existing `lawazim.record` permission (an admin/accountant act), keeping it out of view-only roles without adding a new key. The OMJ remittance uses the separate `lawazim.remit` duty. No new permission keys/module ‚Äî `lawazim.{view,record,remit}` + module `lawazim` were already in the catalog + default roles. | confirm mapping |
| 2026-06-05 | Census reuses the build-step 6 family tree | ¬ß10.2's person-centric family tree is already built (members + relationships, rendered on `/members`). Build-step 8 does NOT rebuild it; census adds snapshots + the ¬ß10.5 economic/welfare fields + approval/progress on top, and reads the existing tree. | confirm reading |
| 2026-06-05 | Census permission duty split | No new permission keys/module needed ‚Äî the catalog already has `census.{view,enter,approve,finalize}` + module `census`. Mapped: `view`=read, `enter`=submit (crowdsourced), `approve`=approve/reject, `finalize`=snapshot lifecycle (open + freeze). So opening a census needs `census.finalize` (President/Super Admin), separating it from day-to-day entry/approval. | confirm mapping |
| 2026-06-05 | Only APPROVED entries count | `summarizeCensusEntries` + the completion % count ONLY `approved` entries (¬ß10.3 "on approval ‚Üí counts in demographics"); pending/rejected never skew the roll-up. A submission is always created `pending` (never auto-approved), and finalising a snapshot freezes it WITHOUT auto-approving the remainder (¬ß3.5). | confirm reading |
| 2026-06-05 | One entry per member per snapshot | A member has at most one entry per snapshot (a partial unique index where `member_id IS NOT NULL`); a re-submission UPDATES that row and RESETS it to `pending` (re-approval required) rather than stacking duplicates or silently keeping a stale approval. New-person entries (`member_id` null) may be many. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Below-living-wage = none/below_15k | The ¬ß10.5 below-living-wage flag is DERIVED from `incomeBand` (`isBelowLivingWage`), with the at/under-line bands = `none` + `below_15k` (coarse PKR bands `none`/`below_15k`/`15k_30k`/`30k_60k`/`above_60k`). Chosen for low-literacy entry; exact figures are never stored. | confirm bands |
| 2026-06-05 | Census progress denominator | Completion % = distinct members with an APPROVED entry √∑ total roster members. The whole roster is the denominator (simple + defensible); new-person submissions are surfaced separately and don't change the denominator. | confirm |
| 2026-06-05 | OMJ sync is a Khundi (tenant) feature | ¬ß22 lists "OMJ Data Sync" under **Khundi Tenant Feature Areas**, so `omj_api_config` + `fetch_conflicts` are TENANT DATA (tenant_id + ¬ß-template RLS) and the queue is per-Khundi. Each Khundi configures its own key and reviews its own conflicts; OMJ-altitude cross-tenant oversight is a later step. | confirm reading |
| 2026-06-05 | Cron = internal timer, not BullMQ | ¬ß4 lists BullMQ; built a dependency-free, self-rescheduling daily timer (02:00 UTC, `unref`'d, self-disables under tests/no-endpoint) so the gates need no live Redis worker. ALL per-tenant-resilient logic is in `runDailySyncAllTenants()` (what the tests exercise), so a BullMQ worker can replace the trigger later with no logic change. | confirm (vs BullMQ now) |
| 2026-06-05 | CNIC matching via in-memory decrypt | CNIC is stored AES-GCM (random IV) so it can't be equality-matched in SQL. The reconcile loads the tenant's members, **decrypts CNICs in memory** (Khundis are small, ¬ß10) to build the match index; plaintext never leaves the server / is never logged. Blind-index column deferred (not needed at this scale). | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Conflict dedup, not stacking | A re-fetch UPDATES the existing PENDING `fetch_conflicts` row for the same person (keyed on `local_member_id` for a conflict, else on `match_value`=cnic‚Äñcard for a `new`) rather than inserting a duplicate (¬ß7.4). `unchanged` records are never queued. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Partial feed never wipes data | `diffIncoming` counts an OPTIONAL field as "changed" only when the OMJ record actually provides a value; `merge` likewise only overwrites fields the feed provides. A sparse feed therefore can't blank out data the Khundi holds (a silent overwrite by omission). STATUS is never changed by a merge (no silent suspend). | confirm reading |
| 2026-06-05 | Resolve semantics | `accept` is valid only for a `new` record (creates a member, provenance `omj_fetch`); `merge` only for a matched `conflict` (updates the local member's identity/demographics); `reject` always valid (no member change). Wrong resolution for the type ‚Üí clean 400. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | API key encryption | The per-tenant OMJ API key is encrypted at rest with the SAME AES-256-GCM field cipher as CNICs (`CnicCipherService`, key from `ENCRYPTION_KEY`, now exported from MembersModule). Never returned (`OmjConfigView.hasApiKey` only) or logged. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | `omj_sync` is a toggleable module | Added module key `omj_sync` (auto-included in `PROVISIONABLE_MODULES`) + keys `omj_sync.{view,config,fetch,resolve}`. Granted to Super Admin (all), General Secretary (all four), Councilor (view/fetch/resolve). | confirm new keys |
| 2026-06-05 | Voting eligibility includes `memberType=member` | ¬ß2.3's literal formula is "active ‚àß male ‚àß 18+". Built `isVotingEligible` as active ‚àß male ‚àß 18+ ‚àß **memberType=member**, because ¬ß2.3 also says a `child` (even a male who turned 18) must be human-confirmed before counting and a `non_member_okhai` is "not a member". So a pending child/non-member is excluded until promoted. Computed on read (age-dependent), never stored. | confirm reading |
| 2026-06-05 | Male child ‚â•18 ‚Üí `pendingVotingActivation` flag | Derived signal (male ‚àß child ‚àß active ‚àß ‚â•18) surfaced for human confirmation; the platform NEVER auto-promotes child‚Üímember or auto-counts them (¬ß2.3, AGENT.md ¬ß3.5). Admin promotes via a normal member edit. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Tenant cannot set `suspended` | Suspension is constitutionally OMJ-altitude (¬ß2.3; `members.suspend` is in `NON_TENANT_KEYS`). The tenant `PATCH /members/:id/status` endpoint refuses `suspended`; the OMJ oversight suspend flow lands in its own build-step. Tenants manage active/inactive/expired. | confirm |
| 2026-06-05 | `member_status_history` carries `tenant_id` | ¬ß7.3 sketches it without one; added `tenant_id` + the RLS template for isolation parity (no tenant-DATA table without RLS). `changed_by` is a bare actor UUID (no FK), mirroring `user_roles.assigned_by`. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Family edges stored BOTH ways | Each relationship writes the edge AND its inverse (PARENT_OF‚ÜîCHILD_OF, SPOUSE_OF/SIBLING_OF symmetric) so the navigable tree (¬ß10.2) resolves from any focal person with one "edges where from=focal" query; add/remove keep the pair in sync; unique `(tenant,from,to,type)`. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | CNIC encryption | A member's CNIC is encrypted at rest with **AES-256-GCM** (`CnicCipherService`), key = SHA-256 of the existing `ENCRYPTION_KEY` placeholder (now REQUIRED at boot). Plaintext CNIC is never returned (absent from `MemberView`) or logged (¬ß17). Reversible (vs. password hashing) because OMJ-sync matching needs it later. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | `households.head_member_id` is 1:1 | Modelled head as a one-to-one (unique) relation ‚Äî a member heads at most one household ‚Äî so Prisma is satisfied and the head FK is unambiguous. Member delete nulls the head (SET NULL), never cascades the household. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | `module_flags` is tenant DATA (has RLS) | Unlike the step-4 authz backbone (no RLS), `module_flags` carries `tenant_id` + the ¬ß-template RLS ‚Äî a tenant's commercial plan must not be readable/writable by another. First tenant-DATA table to reuse the step-2 RLS template. Tenant reads its own flags via `runWithTenant` (gate + SPA menu); Vendor writes cross-tenant via `runAsPlatform`. | confirm design |
| 2026-06-05 | Module default = open | `ModuleEnablementService`: `core` always on; an explicit flag row wins; a MISSING row is treated as ENABLED (default-open) ‚Äî keeps the step-4 seam behaviour and means provisioning explicitly writes rows for the Vendor to toggle. Disabling is the explicit Vendor act that gates a module off. | confirm (vs default-closed) |
| 2026-06-05 | `core` never toggleable | The `core` module (auth/roles/settings) is never stored in `module_flags` and `setModule` refuses to disable it, so a tenant can never lock itself out of administration. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | `tenant.manage` permission | Added a new CORE-module permission `tenant.manage` (PLATFORM scope) for Vendor provisioning + module toggles; excluded from every tenant role (incl. Super Admin) via `NON_TENANT_KEYS`. Granted to Vendor Owner (PLATFORM). | confirm new key |
| 2026-06-05 | Provisioning is atomic + links existing users | `provisionTenant` runs in one `runAsPlatform` tx (tenant‚Üíflags‚Üíroles‚ÜíSuper Admin‚Üíassignment); a person can be Super Admin of multiple Khundis, so an existing OMJ-card holder is LINKED (not duplicated). Default tenant role catalog extracted to `src/provisioning/default-roles.ts` (one source for seed + provisioning). | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Fixed latent step-4 seed bug | `seed.ts` referenced lowercase `RoleAltitude.platform/omj/tenant` (undefined under the `@kc/shared` enum); only survived because the seed runs via `ts-node --transpile-only` and no live DB ran it. Corrected to uppercase members. `prisma/*.ts` is outside the `src/**` typecheck scope ‚Äî consider widening it later. | no (flagging) |
| ‚Äî | Subdomain base | `{tenant}.khundiconnect.com` ‚Äî **CONFIRMED/LOCKED** | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Login credential | **[DECIDE AT BUILD] ‚Üí built BOTH:** OTP-to-phone as the default/primary (low-literacy, ¬ß13.2) AND a password fallback for users who set one. OTP is the recommended path. | yes (confirm OTP-primary is acceptable) |
| 2026-06-05 | Users are global (no RLS) | `users`/`sessions` carry **no `tenant_id` and no RLS** ‚Äî they are platform-global identity; a single human holds stacked roles across tenants/altitudes (¬ß5.5). Tenant/scope binding lives in `user_roles` (step 4). All access via the audited `runAsPlatform` path. | confirm design |
| 2026-06-05 | Authz tables are global (no RLS) | `permissions`/`roles`/`role_permissions`/`user_roles` carry **no RLS** ‚Äî the engine must read a user's STACKED roles across every tenant + platform/omj altitudes to authorize one request (an ALL_TENANTS/PLATFORM grant has null `tenant_context`; RLS-scoping would hide it and break cross-altitude authz). Read on the audited `runAsPlatform` path like `users`. **Tenant isolation is preserved by SCOPE resolution, not RLS on these tables**; every tenant-DATA table still uses the ¬ß-template RLS, and `tenants` RLS stays green (regression). `roles.tenant_id` is an ownership FK, not an isolation boundary. | confirm design |
| 2026-06-05 | Module-enablement seam (step 4 vs 5) | Build-step 4 ships the dual-gate **guards**; the persistent `module_flags` table + Vendor toggle UI are build-step 5 (per ¬ß27). `ModuleEnablementService.isEnabled()` is default-open until step 5 backs it with `module_flags` (no tenant has a reduced plan yet); the GATE's blocking behaviour is proven now by tests. `core` (auth/roles/settings) is always-on/never-toggleable. Step 5 swaps the service body with NO guard/route change. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Scope reach model | Route scopes form a reach order OWN_TENANT<TENANT_SET<ALL_TENANTS<PLATFORM; a granted scope satisfies a required one if it provides ‚â• reach for the target tenant (`scopeSatisfies`). PLATFORM routes need PLATFORM; ALL_TENANTS need ALL_TENANTS/PLATFORM; single-tenant routes accept OWN_TENANT-anchored / TENANT_SET-containing / ALL_TENANTS / PLATFORM. Deny-by-default. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Role time-limit + IP restriction | Implemented from the schema: expired (`time_limited_until`) roles are skipped; a non-empty `ip_restrictions` array requires the requester IP to match (exact-match allow-list; **CIDR matching deferred** as a future enhancement). | confirm (CIDR scope) |
| 2026-06-05 | Session storage | Refresh **sessions persisted in Postgres** (`sessions` table) for durable rotation/revocation/reuse-detection; Redis used for ephemeral OTP + rate-limit. (¬ß4 lists Redis for sessions; chose DB for refresh durability + testability.) | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Token transport | Access token (15m) returned in JSON body, held in memory by the SPA; refresh token (30d) only in an **httpOnly SameSite=Lax cookie** (Secure in prod). Two **distinct** JWT secrets required so a leaked access secret can't mint refresh tokens. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Password hashing | **Node `crypto` scrypt** (memory-hard, no native build dep) rather than bcrypt/argon2 ‚Äî keeps gates runnable anywhere. Params encoded in the hash for future cost bumps. | no |
| 2026-06-05 | Dev seed login users | 6 global identities seeded across altitudes (owner/OMJ/3 tenant admins/1 OTP-only member) with known OMJ card numbers; password users share a **dev-only fixture password** (env-overridable, dev/staging guard, NOT in this public file). Role assignment arrives in step 4. | no |
| ‚Äî | Pricing (PKR) | [DECIDE AT BUILD] ‚Äî placeholder tiers | yes |
| 2026-06-04 | Package manager | **npm workspaces** (not pnpm) so `deploy.sh` runs `npm ci` exactly per ¬ß28.6. `pnpm-workspace.yaml.disabled` documents this. | no |
| 2026-06-04 | Foundation Prisma schema | **Model-free** (datasource+generator only). Tenant tables + RLS are deliberately deferred to build-step 2 so foundation defines no tenant data. `prisma generate` is a no-op until step 2. | no |
| 2026-06-04 | Docker scope (step 1) | `docker-compose.yml` provisions dev **Postgres+Redis** (and CI service containers). App-process Dockerfiles deferred ‚Äî VPS deploy path is **PM2**, not containers (¬ß28.2); untested app images would add risk without value. | no |
| 2026-06-04 | Node version (build env) | Target is **v22** (`.nvmrc`, engines `>=22`). This build/test ran on the sandbox's Node v24; `deploy.sh` warns (does not block) on version drift per ¬ß28.6. | no |
| 2026-06-04 | RLS enforcement model | **GUC-based RLS** with `ENABLE` + `FORCE ROW LEVEL SECURITY`, keyed on transaction-local `app.current_tenant_id`; an explicit `app.bypass_rls='on'` GUC is the single audited cross-tenant path (¬ß5.1). Single `DATABASE_URL` role for operator simplicity ‚Äî **requires the app DB role to be non-superuser / no `BYPASSRLS`** (documented in `docs/MULTITENANCY.md` + `VPS_SETUP.md`), since superusers ignore RLS even with FORCE. | no |
| 2026-06-04 | RLS test infrastructure | Isolation gate uses **PGlite** (Postgres compiled to WASM, in-process) so the test applies the *real* `migration.sql` and exercises genuine RLS with no Docker/superuser. Jest needs `--experimental-vm-modules` (PGlite loads WASM via dynamic import) ‚Äî wired into the api `test` script. | no |
| 2026-06-04 | Step-2 RLS demonstration table | RLS is proven on the **`tenants` registry itself** (a tenant session sees only its own row; cross-tenant read/write denied). The reusable per-table policy template (`tenant_id = app_current_tenant_id()`) is documented for every future tenant-scoped table; those tables + policies arrive with their own build-steps (members in step 6, etc.). | no |
| 2026-06-04 | turbo.json typecheck order | `typecheck` now `dependsOn ["^build","build"]` so Next.js's generated `.next/types` exist/are fresh before `tsc` (prevents a build/typecheck race). Build-tooling only; no runtime/live-path change. | no |
| 2026-06-04 | Reserved subdomain labels | `www`, `staging`, `app`, `api`, `admin` resolve as platform entries (not tenants), so they can never be provisioned as a Khundi subdomain. | confirm list |

### Permanent build-correctness rules (deploy.sh / build config) ‚Äî `feat/25-build-reliability`
Two deploy-blocking bugs were found on staging and fixed permanently (alongside the existing **prisma-generate-before-build** and **npm-ci-include-dev** rules). Both are now enforced by `deploy.sh` and asserted before PM2 restarts, and documented in ARCHITECTURE.md ¬ß28.5/¬ß28.6 + docs/AUTH.md:

1. **API incremental-no-op trap.** `nest build` with `deleteOutDir:true` + `"incremental": true` (in `apps/api/tsconfig.json`) + a leftover `*.tsbuildinfo` = an exit-0 build that wipes `dist/` then emits ZERO files, crashing the API with `Cannot find module './config/env.validation'`. **Fix:** removed `"incremental": true`; `deploy.sh` ¬ß5a now purges `*.tsbuildinfo`, `apps/api/dist`, and the turbo cache (`.turbo`, `node_modules/.cache/turbo`) before building; `turbo.json` build `outputs` include `dist/**` (no more "no output files found" warning). `deploy.sh` ¬ß5c asserts `apps/api/dist/main.js` AND `apps/api/dist/config/env.validation.js` exist, exiting non-zero otherwise so a broken build never restarts PM2.

2. **`NEXT_PUBLIC_*` not baked at build.** `next build` runs with `apps/web` as cwd and reads `.env` from the app dir (not the monorepo-root `.env`); turbo's strict env mode also strips undeclared vars. So a plain `turbo run build` did NOT inline `NEXT_PUBLIC_PLATFORM_BASE_DOMAIN`, silently killing the cross-subdomain login redirect (build-step 24) after deploy. **Fix:** `deploy.sh` ¬ß5b writes an explicit ALLOWLIST (`NEXT_PUBLIC_PLATFORM_BASE_DOMAIN`, `NEXT_PUBLIC_OTP_LOGIN_ENABLED`, `NEXT_PUBLIC_MESSAGING_PROVIDER`) from the sourced `.env` into `apps/web/.env.local` before building; the same vars are declared in `turbo.json` build `env` for cache correctness. **Security:** the allowlist is the boundary ‚Äî server secrets (`DATABASE_URL`, `JWT_*`, `ENCRYPTION_KEY`, `R2_*`) are NEVER copied. ¬ß5c greps `.next/static` to confirm the public value baked in (fail loudly if absent) AND scans for leaked secret values (abort if any found). Verified: clean API build emits `main.js`+`config/env.validation.js`; a plain web build bakes the domain into `.next/static`; no server secret appears in `.next/static`.
